<time>1566226519753<//time><rate>4< /rate><review>This place is such a cute local restaurant, microbrewery, winery. I've been here twice, once for a girls night out and today, for a date night with the hubby.  It's small and they don't take reservations so come early if you don't want to wait. Patio vs inside, I prefer inside since the patio overlooks a parking lot. Free parking in the lot behind the restaurant or free 1 hour parking on the street. They have a nice wine selection from Pozzuoli wine with their vineyard from Paso Robles, I love their Cabernet Sauvignon and Insieme. I've have both the wine sampler and tasting. I prefer the tasting since you can choose what wines. The sampler was ok, love that they served a white wine, Rose, and 2 reds but I only really loved the Rose and one of the reds.... I did enjoy their formaggio (cheese) plate with 4 types of cheese, grapes, hot slices of toasted bread, and olives. It was good, albeit a bit pricey. We fell in love with the goat cheese with chives and onion and bought an extra side for $4 to take home! Their microbrewery has a small but good selection of beer brewed on-site. Today, they were out of some of their beers so my husband tried their Avery White ale which is a guest ale, which was nice and light. They have an in-house honey cream ale which I would love to try next time it's available!

The last time I came here, the girls and I ordered a bruschetta appetizer which was amazing and their pizzas. We ordered an eggplant pizza which was so thinly sliced and fresh and light. Their salad was also delicious. Overall, a cute local spot to hang out, either for girls night, date night, or with friends. I can't wait to introduce more friends to this spot! Love their food, wine, and beer selection!<//review><Pictures>None</Pictures><Response>None<//Response><gmapID>0x80dcdbddb075693f:0x818e094c9dd911f6< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>

<userid>114045244660912465753</userid>< name>
Aaron Morris<//name>
< date>
1430269366171<//date>
< rate>
5<//rate>
< Text>
Big news for beer and wine drinkers in Tustin. Centro, a winery and microbrewery, is now open in Old Town Tustin.

The brewery-restaurant is owned by Pozzuoli Vineyard & Winery, which is located in Paso Robles. (How often do you see a winery that lists its two locations as someplace in wine country, and Tustin?) Pazzuoli opened a tasting room in Tustin a couple of years ago at 15481 Red Hill Avenue, and now has opened this impressive location in Old Town Tustin.

I'm a wine fan, but what really got me excited about this place is the microbrewery. They call the beer side of the operation Archaic Craft Brewery. I visited on opening day, and they had four beers on tap, but only one was created in house, and that was the Honey Kolsch. If the Honey Kolsch is any indication of the brews we can expect from Archaic, then this place will be great for beer drinkers. It was a great German style Kolsch, with good mouth feel and no harsh aftertaste.

This is a true family business, with Enrico Pozzuoli as the winemaker, and his son Sandro Pozzuoli handling the brewmaster duties. I spent some time with Sandro discussing the beers he is brewing. His knowledge was apparent, and I was impressed that, even though he wanted to roll out a beer or two more for the grand opening, he held back because they weren't yet where he wanted them to be. Look for an IPA soon.

I'm hoping they will expand the number of available beers on tap. Certainly, if they want to make this a destination for microbrewery crawlers, they'll need a greater selection. But how many beers can you really drink? For now, live with four, and go to Centro to check out the impressive modern/rustic interior.

As to the food, we tried the Margherita pizza ($9) and the Hummus plate ($8) (we dug into hummus plate so quickly, we forgot to take a picture; picture above shows cheese plate ordered by another patron). Both were excellent. The pizzas are baked in a wood-fired oven. They also offer cheese plates, salads, paninis, and desserts.

Beers were $6 and $7 a pint, and the wine ranged from $10 to $15 a glass. Personal pizzas cost about $10 to $14. Some pizza is available by the slice for $4. If you like the beer, you can take a 32 or 64-ounce growler to go.

Centro is a great addition to Old Town Tustin. Be sure to give it a try.< /Text>

What a peaceful spot full of zen vibes. There is a hike trail going up and you can find the cute little waterfall and LA views. Coming back again to continue trail up.<//text>

Wow!üòÅ My dentist, Dr. Hinh at Sac Dentist (formerly Laurel Hills), is AHHmazing. He has the most state-of-the-art Covid protocols I've ever heard of. Dental Assistants & Hygienists are grateful to work there. Here's a glimpse:

ü¶∑ Night before: You receive an auto form via text to complete about your health.
ü¶∑ Morning of: You receive a text to click on when you arrive, & they'll meet you at the door.
ü¶∑ This text also includes the same survey about your health.
ü¶∑ A person wearing full PPE greets you at the door & takes your temperature.
ü¶∑ Plexiglass surrounds the receptionists.
ü¶∑ You're escorted to your room, where you wash your hands & rinse w/a germicidal rinse.
ü¶∑ Your last xrays are loaded & visible on a large flat screen. Trays are sanitized & ready.
ü¶∑ Each room has it's own hepafilter room purifier, plus the entire facility has one.
ü¶∑ They provide you w/a spot to place your mask/items that is sanitized between patients.
ü¶∑ The person working on my teeth has on a surgeon's cap, an N95 AND surgical mask, a face shield, gown, & special gloves.
ü¶∑ They provide you w/a pair of sanitized &  shaded goggles to protect your eyes!
ü¶∑ You're seated & they ask about your health.
ü¶∑ They do a full mouth inspection for disease.
ü¶∑ They place a small, soft, rubbery, green, leaf-shaped üçÉ suction tube in the side of your mouth for the duration of the visit.
ü¶∑ During the polishing & flossing segment of my visit, they also bend a tall, wide, crane-like stationary vacuum hose near my mouth, to capture any droplets.ü¶ï
ü¶∑ My Dental Hygienist --Mattie-- is a gem.üíé She had to check my gum marginsüò≥ & it was painless.üíû They use special technology, too.

ü¶∑ At the end, they give you a parting gift that includes a colorful zip pouch w/a toothbrush, floss, & toothpaste. ü§ó
ü¶∑ My Dentist came in for an exam, also in full PPE. He's cheerful, kind, & gentle. The best. üèÜ
ü¶∑ I love this place! ü•∞üíû#Number1Dentist!</Text>

The process was smooth and quick as most of the paperwork had been completed online.  The dealership is new and spacious.
